var headerBidderBack = [];
function headerBidderBackInitialize(tmp_ads_app) {
	headerBidderBack[tmp_ads_app] = [];
	headerBidderBack[tmp_ads_app]['called_to_render'] = false;
	headerBidderBack[tmp_ads_app]['prebid'] = false;
	headerBidderBack[tmp_ads_app]['a9'] = false;
}
function headerBidderBackMethod(bidder, tmp_ads_app) {
        headerBidderBack[tmp_ads_app][bidder] = true;
        if((headerBidderBack[tmp_ads_app]['prebid'] === true) && (headerBidderBack[tmp_ads_app]['a9'] === true)){
		  eval(('showSlot_' + (tmp_ads_app.replace(/-/g, '_') + '_prebid')))(tmp_ads_app);
		}
    }

	function ytAdActivate() { isYTAdActive = 1; goThroughSlots();}
	function ytAdDeactivate() { isYTAdActive = 0;}
    var isInViewport = function (elem,tmp_ads_app) {		
		if((tmp_ads_app.indexOf("adhesive_oop") > -1) && (adAdhesive_1.indexOf(tmp_ads_app) > -1)){return true;}
		var bounding = elem.getBoundingClientRect();
		var boundary_top_operator = "bounding.top >= 0";
		if((tmp_ads_app == "ad-list-inimage1") || (tmp_ads_app == "ad-list-inimage2") || (tmp_ads_app == "ad-list-inimage3") || (tmp_ads_app == "ad-list-inimage4") || (tmp_ads_app == "ad-list-inimage5") || (tmp_ads_app == "ad-list-inimage6") || (tmp_ads_app == "ad-inarticle-long-btf3")  || (tmp_ads_app == "ad-inarticle-long-btf4")  || (tmp_ads_app == "ad-inarticle-long-btf5")  || (tmp_ads_app == "ad-inarticle-long-btf6")  || (tmp_ads_app == "ad-inarticle-long-btf7")  || (tmp_ads_app == "ad-inarticle-long-btf8")){
		  boundary_top_operator = "bounding.top > 0";
		}
		if(adSlotsRenderedArray.indexOf(tmp_ads_app) > -1){
			return (
				isYTAdActive == 1 &&
				eval(boundary_top_operator) &&
				//bounding.left >= 0 &&
				bounding.bottom <= ((window.innerHeight || document.documentElement.clientHeight)) //&&
				//bounding.right <= (window.innerWidth || document.documentElement.clientWidth)
			);
		}else{
			return (
				isYTAdActive == 1 &&
				eval(boundary_top_operator) &&
				//bounding.left >= 0 &&
				bounding.bottom <= ((window.innerHeight || document.documentElement.clientHeight)+700) //&&
				//bounding.right <= (window.innerWidth || document.documentElement.clientWidth)
			);
		}		
	};
	function refreshPrebidAdSlot(slot, ind){
		adSlotsArray[ind] = slot;
		goThroughSlots();
	}
	function goThroughSlots(){ 
		for (var i = 0; i < adSlotsArray.length; i++) {
			if(adSlotsArray[i] != ""){
			var adSlotDiv = document.getElementById(adSlotsArray[i]);
			if(!adSlotDiv){
			  adSlotsArray[adSlotsArray.indexOf(adSlotsArray[i])] = "";
			}else{
			  if ((window_w >= 768) && (adSlotsArray[i] == "ad-leaderboard-mobile")) {
				adSlotsArray[adSlotsArray.indexOf(adSlotsArray[i])] = "";
			  } else if ((window_w >= 768) && (adSlotsArray[i].indexOf("article-box-350top") > -1)) {
				adSlotsArray[adSlotsArray.indexOf(adSlotsArray[i])] = "";			  
			  } else if (!((window.innerWidth <= 980) || (navigator.mobile)) && (adSlotsArray[i].indexOf("adhesive_oop") > -1)) {			
  			    adSlotsArray[adSlotsArray.indexOf(adSlotsArray[i])] = "";
			  } else if ((window_w >= 768) && (adSlotsArray[i].indexOf("ad-between-block-mo") > -1)) {
				adSlotsArray[adSlotsArray.indexOf(adSlotsArray[i])] = "";
			  } else if ((window_w < 768) && (adSlotsArray[i].indexOf("ad-in-leaderboard1") > -1)) {
				adSlotsArray[adSlotsArray.indexOf(adSlotsArray[i])] = "";
			  } else if ((window_w < 768)  && (adSlotsArray[i].indexOf("ad-leaderboard") > -1) && (adSlotsArray[i] != "ad-leaderboard-mobile")) {
				adSlotsArray[adSlotsArray.indexOf(adSlotsArray[i])] = "";
			  } else if ((window_w >= 768) && (adSlotsArray[i] == "ad-atf")) {
				adSlotsArray[adSlotsArray.indexOf(adSlotsArray[i])] = "";
			  } else if ((window_w <= 1024) && (adSlotsArray[i] == "ad-category_350")) {
				adSlotsArray[adSlotsArray.indexOf(adSlotsArray[i])] = "";
			  } else{
				if(isInViewport(adSlotDiv,adSlotsArray[i])){
				var tmp_ads_app = adSlotsArray[i];
				var lazyload_appnexus_offered_reloaded=1;
				if(adSlotsRenderedArray.indexOf(tmp_ads_app) == -1){adSlotsRenderedArray.push(tmp_ads_app);lazyload_appnexus_offered_reloaded=0;}/*if((!yt_is_mobile) && (tmp_ads_app.indexOf("ad-leaderboard") == -1)){window.setTimeout(refreshPrebidAdSlot, 50000, adSlotsArray[adSlotsArray.indexOf(adSlotsArray[i])],adSlotsArray.indexOf(adSlotsArray[i]));}*/
				adSlotsArray[adSlotsArray.indexOf(adSlotsArray[i])] = "";if(allowAmazonHeaderBidder(tmp_ads_app)){
									headerBidderBackInitialize(tmp_ads_app);
									pbjs.que.push(function() {
										pbjs.requestBids({
											adUnitCodes: [tmp_ads_app],
											bidsBackHandler: eval(("var_" + (tmp_ads_app.replace(/-/g, '_')+'_prebid')))
										});
									});									
									if((tmp_ads_app == "ad-leaderboard") || (tmp_ads_app == "ad-leaderboard-mobile") || ((window_w < 768) && ((tmp_ads_app == "ad-atf") || (tmp_ads_app == "article-box-350top")))){
										apstag.fetchBids({
											slots: apstagGetSlot(tmp_ads_app),
											timeout: PREBID_TIMEOUT_FIRST_AD
										}, function(bids) {
											headerBidderBackMethod("a9", bids[0].slotID);
										});
										window.setTimeout(eval(("showSlot_" + (tmp_ads_app.replace(/-/g, "_") + "_prebid"))), PREBID_TIMEOUT_FIRST_AD,tmp_ads_app);
									}else{
										apstag.fetchBids({
											slots: apstagGetSlot(tmp_ads_app),
											timeout: PREBID_TIMEOUT
										}, function(bids) {
											headerBidderBackMethod("a9", bids[0].slotID);
										});
										window.setTimeout(eval(("showSlot_" + (tmp_ads_app.replace(/-/g, "_") + "_prebid"))), PREBID_TIMEOUT,tmp_ads_app);
									}									
								  }else{
									pbjs.que.push(function() {
									 if((tmp_ads_app == "ad-leaderboard") || (tmp_ads_app == "ad-leaderboard-mobile") || ((window_w < 768) && ((tmp_ads_app == "ad-atf") || (tmp_ads_app == "article-box-350top")))){
										pbjs.requestBids({
										   timeout: PREBID_TIMEOUT_FIRST_AD,
										   adUnitCodes: [tmp_ads_app],
										   bidsBackHandler: eval(("showSlot_" + (tmp_ads_app.replace(/-/g, '_')+'_prebid')))
										 });
									 }else{
										pbjs.requestBids({
										   timeout: PREBID_TIMEOUT,
										   adUnitCodes: [tmp_ads_app],
										   bidsBackHandler: eval(("showSlot_" + (tmp_ads_app.replace(/-/g, '_')+'_prebid')))
										 });
									 }									 
									});
								  }}
			  }
			}
		}
		}
	}for (var i = 0; i < adSlotsArray.length; i++) {
    if(allowAmazonHeaderBidder(adSlotsArray[i])){
		eval("function showSlot_"+adSlotsArray[i].replace(/-/g, '_')+'_prebid'+"(tmp_ads_app){if(headerBidderBack[tmp_ads_app]['called_to_render'] === false){headerBidderBack[tmp_ads_app]['called_to_render'] = true;apstag.setDisplayBids(['" + adSlotsArray[i] + "']);pbjs.setTargetingForGPTAsync(['" + adSlotsArray[i] + "']);googletag.pubads().refresh([eval('" + adSlotsArray[i] + "'.replace(/-/g, '_')+'_prebid')]);}}");
		eval("function var_"+adSlotsArray[i].replace(/-/g, '_')+'_prebid'+"(){headerBidderBackMethod('prebid', '" + adSlotsArray[i] + "');}");
	}else{
		eval("function showSlot_"+adSlotsArray[i].replace(/-/g, '_')+'_prebid'+"(){pbjs.setTargetingForGPTAsync(['"+adSlotsArray[i]+"']);googletag.pubads().refresh([eval('"+adSlotsArray[i]+"'.replace(/-/g, '_')+'_prebid')]);}");
	}

   <script>
    // Used to defer the loading of stylesheets.
  function loadStyleSheet(src) {
    if (document.createStyleSheet) {
      document.createStyleSheet(src);
    }
    else {
      var stylesheet = document.createElement('link');
      stylesheet.href = src;
      stylesheet.rel = 'stylesheet';
      stylesheet.type = 'text/css';
      document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild(stylesheet);
    }
  }
   </script>

    var accItem = document.getElementsByClassName('accordionItem');
    var accHD = document.getElementsByClassName('accordionItemHeading');
    for (i = 0; i < accHD.length; i++) {
        accHD[i].addEventListener('click', toggleItem, false);
    }
    function toggleItem() {
        var itemClass = this.parentNode.className;
        for (i = 0; i < accItem.length; i++) {
            accItem[i].className = 'accordionItem closed';
        }
        if (itemClass == 'accordionItem closed') {
            this.parentNode.className = 'accordionItem open';
        }
    }
